        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer700348357" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12550229717564109105">LOVED this book!! What's not to love??? Basically a MG re-working of "Charlie and the Chocolate Factory" but with an eccentric game maker and set in a LIBRARY!!! Not just any library either, but a state of the art, amazing, magnificent library with holograms, digital ceilings, mag lev lifts to retrieve books shelved high in the air, a gaming room and food! I really, really, really want to go to Mr. Lemoncello's library! Peppered with fun puzzles, anagrams, rubrics and literally DOZENS of literat</span>
  <span id="freeText12550229717564109105" style="display:none">LOVED this book!! What's not to love??? Basically a MG re-working of "Charlie and the Chocolate Factory" but with an eccentric game maker and set in a LIBRARY!!! Not just any library either, but a state of the art, amazing, magnificent library with holograms, digital ceilings, mag lev lifts to retrieve books shelved high in the air, a gaming room and food! I really, really, really want to go to Mr. Lemoncello's library! Peppered with fun puzzles, anagrams, rubrics and literally DOZENS of literature references, this is a young bibliophile's dream book. While this book will have HUGE appeal among librarians and young book lovers, I also think that it is entertaining enough to keep just about anyone reading. Do I smell a Newberry? I certainly hope so as this one is pure fun with a lot of information sneakily thrown in. Kids will be absorbing information about the Dewey Decimal system and library organization and barely even know it! Heee heeee heeee... sneaky Chris Grabenstein! Highly recommended for grades 3 - 6... not sure of its appeal for older middle graders. It might seem a little too young for them.</span>
  <a data-text-id="12550229717564109105" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer17255579723282791467">This is a kind of a new twist on Willy Wonka and the Chocolate Factory but better because it's in a library.   <span id="freeText17255579723282791467" style="display:none">This is a kind of a new twist on Willy Wonka and the Chocolate Factory but better because it's in a library. I want to say that I not much of a middle grade reader but I am trying to get my kids to love reading and I am rereading some books that I loved as a kid. I say this on the library website and it seemed fascinating to me so I thought I would give it a short. I loved the characters and the games but my favorite was all the literary figures, authors, and books, that were worked into the story. It was also so much fun solving the puzzles in the books and made the story move very quickly. I would recommend for middle grade but also a fun light read for adults.<br /><br /><a href="http://thebookreturn.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">My blog</a></span>

<div id="review_1578888172" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1578888172" />
    <a title="C." class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/10501026-c"><img alt="C." src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1578542204p2/10501026.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1578888172?book_show_action=true">Mar 13, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="C." class="user" itemprop="url" name="C." href="/user/show/10501026-c">C.</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10501026-c?shelf=riedel-titles-2016">riedel-titles-2016</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1578888172" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12676533793063096517">I relish creativity, the bravery to make-up possibilities! I am amazed at how much fun this novel is; a writer appreciative of exciting stories. Dialogue sped naturally. We needn’t care about phrases being au-courant. I never compare literature to berate it. There is no ownership on a whacky adventure. I would cherish this kind of extravaganza! I love “<b>Escape From Mr. Lemoncello’s Library</b>” on its own merits, which are numerous. I venture to describe this story as: a younger, non-sullen <i>“The Brea</i></span>
  <span id="freeText12676533793063096517" style="display:none">I relish creativity, the bravery to make-up possibilities! I am amazed at how much fun this novel is; a writer appreciative of exciting stories. Dialogue sped naturally. We needn’t care about phrases being au-courant. I never compare literature to berate it. There is no ownership on a whacky adventure. I would cherish this kind of extravaganza! I love “<b>Escape From Mr. Lemoncello’s Library</b>” on its own merits, which are numerous. I venture to describe this story as: a younger, non-sullen <i>“The Breakfast Club”</i> and an urban, non-dangerous <i>“The Goonies”</i>!<br /><br />Our protagonist is youngest of three brothers: good at video and board games but no match for them elsewhere. Readers root for Kyle to shine and he is honoured to discover that his brothers always considered him a team mate. We have a brainy reader who becomes admired by a new gaggle of friends and a girl whose family needed money but who felt good about putting friends first. <i>“The Breakfast Club”</i> bonding refers to peers who had not been buddies before; seeing schoolmates in a new light. <i>“The Goonies”</i> flavour of course, is this once-in-a-lifetime quest: each child using their talent and knowledge to solve clue after clue, culminating in a triumphant end-game.<br /><br />Being able to speak to a departed, beloved librarian was touching. I was especially moved by the way Kyle’s heart leaped, because he could treat his whole family to a gift card! It’s wonderful seeing bookworm Sierra’s knowledge blossom into friendships and Kyle beginning to read. Imagine the wonderment of having free reign of a place, to brainstorm clues with friends and solve a highly-rewarding quest! It pays off, that <b>Chris Grabenstein</b> let himself carry zany ideas and Mr. Lemoncello’s personality, all the way! This cache of puzzles motivates us to think and to seek possibilities everywhere.</span>
  <a data-text-id="12676533793063096517" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('xAthT0F0d6EZ9jZbn4tjv5cIRFUjq34kjGkpOSGBTdEms8O0tFC+bYmHWeY3TsO8njn8BXN1fMtC/sIDa0Dvjg==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('ZLRQlLKHh/cOMOPVPH+9qnKj00NJez6eBaQozFw2vCeGDPJvR6NOO55BjGiUuh2pe5JrExmlPHHLM8P2FvceeA==')})
  }

Mr. Lemoncello is thinking about his legacy, and whichever player finds the ticket will be the first to win a spot in an elite group of kids who will compete in the next books to win Mr. Lemoncello\'s ENTIRE EMPIRE!\n\n* &quot;A worthy successor to . . .
